       <article class="content-wrapper wrapper clearfix detail-graphic detail-feature" id="article-36571">
        <header class="content-header">
         <h1>
          The Pros And Cons Of Going Vegetarian
         </h1>
        </header>
        <main class="content-body large-thing" data-area="Article Body">
         <div class="content-masthead">
         </div>
         <div class="content-meta small-thing">
          <div>
           <a class="content-type" data-track-action="Meta: Feature Type" data-track-category="Article" data-track-label="/search?tags=" href="/features/infographic">
            INFOGRAPHIC
           </a>
           <span class="content-published">
            July 29, 2014
           </span>
          </div>
          <div>
           <span class="content-issue">
            <a data-track-action="Meta: Issue" data-track-category="Article" data-track-label="/issue/5030/" href="/issue/5030/">
             Vol 50 Issue 30
            </a>
            <span class="bul">
             
            </span>
           </span>
           <span class="content-tags">
            <a data-track-action="Meta: Tags" data-track-category="Article" data-track-label="/tag/food" href="/tag/food">
             Food
            </a>
            <span class="bul">
             
            </span>
            <a data-track-action="Meta: Tags" data-track-category="Article" data-track-label="/tag/health" href="/tag/health">
             Health
            </a>
            <span class="bul">
             
            </span>
            <a data-track-action="Meta: Tags" data-track-category="Article" data-track-label="/tag/fitness" href="/tag/fitness">
             Fitness
            </a>
            <span class="bul">
             
            </span>
            <a data-track-action="Meta: Tags" data-track-category="Article" data-track-label="/tag/lifestyle" href="/tag/lifestyle">
             Lifestyle
            </a>
           </span>
          </div>
          <div class="article-share-tools share-container">
           <div class="share-tools share-widget" data-share-description="While the vast majority of Americans are meat eaters, USDA statistics show that a growing number of Americans are becoming vegetarians and vegans to adopt healthier diets, ensure food safety, and practice ethical eating habits." data-share-image="http://i.onionstatic.com/onion/2690/1/16x9/1200.jpg" data-share-redirect-url="http://www.theonion.com/fb-close" data-share-title="The Pros And Cons Of Going Vegetarian" data-share-url="http://www.theonion.com/r/36571">
            <a class="share-facebook button" data-action="Facebook share clicked" data-track-action="Meta: Share" data-track-category="Article" data-track-label="Facebook" href="#" target="_blank" title="Share via Facebook">
             <i class="fa fa-facebook fa-fw">
             </i>
            </a>
            <a class="share-twitter button" data-action="Twitter share clicked" data-track-action="Meta: Share" data-track-category="Article" data-track-label="Twitter" href="#" title="Share via Twitter">
             <i class="fa fa-twitter fa-fw">
             </i>
            </a>
            <a class="share-mail button" data-action="Email share clicked" data-track-action="Meta: Share" data-track-category="Article" data-track-label="Email" href="#" title="Share via Email">
             <i class="fa fa-envelope fa-fw">
             </i>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="dfp dfp-slot-article-button" data-ad-unit="article-button" data-targeting='{"dfp_pagetype": "article", "dfp_content_id": 36571}'>
          </div>
         </div>
         <div class="large-thing content-main">
          <div class="content-media on-trigger-overlay">
           <div class="image" data-crop="original" data-image-id="26901" data-type="image">
            <div>
            </div>
            <noscript>
             <img src="http://i.onionstatic.com/onion/2690/1/original/600.jpg"/>
            </noscript>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="on-overlay on-overlay-scale">
           <button class="on-overlay-close" type="button">
            Close
           </button>
           <figure class="content-image original">
            <img alt="" src="http://i.onionstatic.com/onion/2690/1/original/1200.jpg"/>
           </figure>
          </div>
          <div class="content-text">
           <div>
            <p>
             <b>
              While the vast majority of Americans are meat eaters, USDA statistics show that a growing number of Americans are becoming vegetarians and vegans to adopt healthier diets, ensure food safety, and practice ethical eating habits. Here are some of the pros and cons of going vegetarian:
             </b>
            </p>
            <p>
             <b>
              PROS
             </b>
            </p>
            <ul>
             <li>
              Are still allowed to smell, feel, and look at meat
             </li>
             <li>
              Get to declare I cant eat this! while throwing a meat dish on the floor
             </li>
             <li>
              Tofu can be substituted in any non-vegetarian recipe calling for bland, flavorless chunks
             </li>
             <li>
              Help replace environmentally harmful livestock industry with the environmentally harmful agriculture industry
             </li>
             <li>
              Can enjoy unadulterated pleasure of slowly masticating bitter leaves and grasses
             </li>
             <li>
              Fewer heart attacks than last year
             </li>
             <li>
              Rewards points
             </li>
             <li>
              Subtle nods of approval from every passing animal
             </li>
             <li>
              Increased energy for complaining about how shitty life is now
             </li>
            </ul>
            <p>
             <b>
              CONS
             </b>
            </p>
            <ul>
             <li>
              Beef, pork, and chicken all contain meat, and you will not be allowed to eat them
             </li>
             <li>
              Have to perfect the forced smile that accompanies choking down tempeh
             </li>
             <li>
              May lose the weight, high cholesterol, and saturated fats you worked so hard for over the years
             </li>
             <li>
              Get constantly pestered with questions from fascinated acquaintances
             </li>
             <li>
              Will be forced to resign as vice president of your local Gravy Club
             </li>
             <li>
              Could become the kind of person who asks questions about soups
             </li>
             <li>
              No matter how many vegetables you scarf down, you will never get your picture mounted on the wall of a steakhouse
             </li>
             <li>
              Many animals not slaughtered for consumption could go on to live long lives filled with heartbreak and disappointment
             </li>
             <li>
              Can go back to eating meat at any time without any consequence whatsoever
             </li>
            </ul>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="below-article-tools">
           <div class="share-container">
